[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Movie)

:   "*The shroud of the dark side has fallen. Begun, the Clone War has.*"
:   ―Yoda[[1]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones-1)

***Star Wars*: Episode II *Attack of the Clones*** is a [2002](/wiki/2002 "2002") film directed by [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas") & written by Lucas and [Jonathan Hales](/wiki/Jonathan_Hales "Jonathan Hales"). It is the second part of the *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* [prequel trilogy](/wiki/Prequel_trilogy "Prequel trilogy").

The film is set ten years after the [Battle of Naboo](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo"), when [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") is on the brink of civil war. Under the leadership of renegade [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Count](/wiki/Count "Count") [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku"), thousands of systems threaten to secede from the [Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"). When an assassination attempt is made on Senator [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala"), the former [Queen](/wiki/Queen "Queen") of [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo"), Jedi apprentice [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") is assigned to protect her. In contrast, his mentor [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") is assigned to investigate the assassination attempt. Soon, the Jedi are drawn into the heart of the [Separatist](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") [movement](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis"), and the beginning of a new threat to the galaxy: the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars").

*Attack of the Clones* was the first *Star Wars* film to use a high-definition [digital 24-frame](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/24p "wikipedia:24p") system for most of its live-action scenes. The film was a financial success, grossing over $600 million at the worldwide box office. However, for the first time, a *Star Wars* film did not earn the highest box-office sales for the year; *Attack of the Clones* ended up fourth behind *[The Lord of the Rings: The Two Towers](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Lord_of_the_Rings:_The_Two_Towers "wikipedia:The Lord of the Rings: The Two Towers")*, *[Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets_(film) "wikipedia:Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (film)")*, and *[Spider-Man](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spider-Man_(2002_film) "wikipedia:Spider-Man (2002 film)")*.

## Opening crawl[]

| Episode II ATTACK OF THE CLONES |
| --- |
| ``` There is unrest in the Galactic Senate. Several thousand solar systems have declared their intentions to leave the Republic.  This separatist movement, under the leadership of the mysterious Count Dooku, has made it difficult for the limited number of Jedi Knights to maintain peace and order in the galaxy.  Senator Amidala, the former Queen of Naboo, is returning to the Galactic Senate to vote on the critical issue of creating an ARMY OF THE REPUBLIC to assist the overwhelmed Jedi.... ``` |
|  |

## Plot summary[]

Ten years after the events of  [*The Phantom Menace*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace "Star Wars: Episode I The Phantom Menace"), the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic") is in crisis. A [Separatist movement](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") led by former [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Count](/wiki/Count "Count") [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku"), alias the [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Tyranus, is threatening the peace, causing the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate") to debate a [Military Creation Act](/wiki/Military_Creation_Act "Military Creation Act") to form a standing army for the Republic's protection. [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala"), former [Queen](/wiki/Queen "Queen") of [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo"), intends to return to the Senate and vote against the Act, even though there are no longer enough Jedi to maintain peace and justice in [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy").

 [![ and  chase  through .](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/Attack_of_the_clones_1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090918165459) [![ and  chase  through .](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/Attack_of_the_clones_1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20090918165459)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/23/Attack_of_the_clones_1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090918165459) 

[Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") and [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") chase [Zam Wesell](/wiki/Zam_Wesell "Zam Wesell") through [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant").

 

Upon her arrival on [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant"), she narrowly escapes an [assassination attempt](/wiki/Plot_to_assassinate_Senator_Amidala "Plot to assassinate Senator Amidala") that claims the life of her decoy, [Cordé](/wiki/Cord%C3%A9 "Cordé"). As a result, [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") [Sheev Palpatine](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") requests that [Jedi Knight](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi") and his apprentice, [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), protect her.

That night, the assassin [Zam Wesell](/wiki/Zam_Wesell "Zam Wesell") makes another attempt on Amidala's life, though the Jedi are able to foil her plot. They pursue her through [Galactic City](/wiki/Imperial_City "Imperial City"), eventually disarming her in the [Outlander Club](/wiki/Outlander_Club "Outlander Club"). Upon being questioned by Obi-Wan and Anakin outside the bar, she is killed by a [saberdart](/wiki/Kamino_saberdart "Kamino saberdart"), fired by a [mysterious man](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett"), before the Jedi can learn the name of her employer. Returning to the [Jedi Temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace"), Obi-Wan is assigned by [the council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council") to track down the assassin's killer. Meanwhile, Anakin continues his task of protecting the Senator and is asked to escort her back to her home planet of Naboo. Anakin welcomes the opportunity, as he often becomes angry and frustrated by Obi-Wan's criticism and is glad to have an opportunity to be on his own. Further, he has become infatuated with Padmé and relishes the chance to spend time with her. [Junior Representative](/wiki/Junior_Representative "Junior Representative") [Jar Jar Binks](/wiki/Jar_Jar_Binks "Jar Jar Binks") assumes Amidala's duties in her absence, despite the Senator being mad at not being at the Senate when the [fate](/wiki/Destiny "Destiny") of the Military Creation Act is decided.

 [![Obi-Wan engages  on .](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/JangoVSKenobiAOTC.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160129224924) [![Obi-Wan engages  on .](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/JangoVSKenobiAOTC.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160129224924)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/JangoVSKenobiAOTC.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160129224924) 

Obi-Wan engages [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett") on [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino").

 

During the investigation into the assassination attempt on Amidala, Obi-Wan is led to a mysterious planet called [Kamino](/wiki/Kamino "Kamino")—missing from the [Jedi Archives](/wiki/Jedi_Archives "Jedi Archives")—where he discovers a secret [clone army](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic") being developed for the Republic. He is told by [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister "Prime Minister") [Lama Su](/wiki/Lama_Su "Lama Su") that the military was ordered almost ten [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") ago by Jedi Master [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas "Sifo-Dyas")—although Obi-Wan was "under the impression" that Sifo-Dyas was killed before that time. A [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") named Jango Fett was hired as the template for the clones. Obi-Wan meets Jango on Kamino and believes him to be the killer he has been tracking. He tries to capture Jango, which leads to a titanic one-on-one fight between them. Jango makes use of his blasters and missile equipment, managing to defeat Obi-Wan by sending him plummeting into the raging sea below. Thinking he is dead, Jango departs Kamino with his son [Boba](/wiki/Boba_Fett "Boba Fett"). Unable to capture Jango, Obi-Wan places a [homing beacon](/wiki/Homing_beacon "Homing beacon") on his ship, *[Slave I](/wiki/Slave_I "Slave I")*, and follows him to the planet of [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis").

 [![Anakin and  spend time on .](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/Attack_of_the_clones_3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160129221934) [![Anakin and  spend time on .](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/Attack_of_the_clones_3.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160129221934)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7e/Attack_of_the_clones_3.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160129221934) 

Anakin and [Padmé](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala") spend time on [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo").

 

Meanwhile, Anakin and Padmé have been spending much time together on Naboo, enjoying each other's company and playfully frolicking in the fields. Eventually, Anakin reveals his deep love for her, vowing to do whatever she requests. However, Padmé resists, explaining that it would be impossible for the two of them to be together since she is a Senator and he is a Jedi. Anakin is angered by this and experiences inner conflict between his strong desires for her and his duties as a Jedi.

Anakin is also troubled by a newfound sense that [his mother](/wiki/Shmi_Skywalker_Lars "Shmi Skywalker Lars") is in grave danger, and he beckons for Padmé to accompany him to his home planet of [Tatooine](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine")—in the process, disobeying Obi-Wan's orders to remain on Naboo. Upon arriving, Anakin tracks down his former owner [Watto](/wiki/Watto "Watto"), from whom he learns that his mother has married a [moisture farmer](/wiki/Moisture_farmer "Moisture farmer") named [Cliegg Lars](/wiki/Cliegg_Lars "Cliegg Lars"), and travels to the [Lars moisture farm](/wiki/Lars_homestead "Lars homestead"). There, Anakin and Padmé find [C-3PO](/wiki/C-3PO "C-3PO"), and the droid introduces Anakin to his step-brother [Owen](/wiki/Owen_Lars "Owen Lars"). Cliegg tells Anakin the horrible truth that his mother was kidnapped a month ago by a pack of [Tusken Raiders](/wiki/Tusken_Raider "Tusken Raider"). Anakin travels through the night and finds her tied and beaten in a [Tusken camp](/wiki/Unidentified_Tusken_village "Unidentified Tusken village"). Within moments, she dies in his arms. Enraged and heartbroken, he massacres the Tusken community: men, women, and even children. On Coruscant, [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") senses a terrible darkness in [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force") as the slaughter continues ([Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn "Qui-Gon Jinn")'s voice shouts "Anakin, Anakin, no!" during this scene). Anakin then brings his mother's body back to the homestead, where her funeral is held.

On Geonosis, Obi-Wan overhears a meeting between Count Dooku and the leaders of the commerce guilds and learns that they are behind the separatist movement and have built up a [new droid army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army"). He also knows that it was [Nute Gunray](/wiki/Nute_Gunray "Nute Gunray") who ordered the assassination of Amidala as revenge for the defeat of the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation") at the [Battle of Naboo](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo"). Obi-Wan transmits his findings to the Council, relayed by way of Anakin and Padmé's ship, though he is surrounded by [droidekas](/wiki/Droideka "Droideka") and captured before he can finish his report.

 [![The ](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/Battle_of_Geonosis.png/revision/latest?cb=20170325151752) [![The ](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/Battle_of_Geonosis.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170325151752)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/Battle_of_Geonosis.png/revision/latest?cb=20170325151752) 

The [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis")

 

Now that the Jedi council knows of Dooku's army, Jedi Master [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu") leads a [battalion](/wiki/Jedi_assault_team "Jedi assault team") of Jedi to Geonosis. Unbeknownst to them, Anakin and Padmé also make their way there to rescue Obi-Wan. Meanwhile, Representative Binks calls for Chancellor Palpatine to be given emergency powers, with which he can reach the recently discovered clone army into battle.

Back on Geonosis, Count Dooku tries to persuade Obi-Wan to join him, using the fact that he was once Qui-Gon's master, that Qui-Gon, if alive, would have joined Dooku and that the Republic and Jedi have lost their ways and must be fought against. Obi-Wan refuses to join Dooku, saying that Dooku is wrong about the Republic and Jedi losing their ways and that Qui-Gon would have never joined Dooku if Qui-Gon was alive. Anakin and Padmé arrive on the planet but are quickly captured by Jango Fett and sentenced to death, joining Obi-Wan in the [Geonosis arena](/wiki/Petranaki_Arena "Petranaki Arena"), where they are to be executed. Moments before heading outside, Padame and Anakin confess their love to each other. In the high stands, Count Dooku, Nute Gunray, [Rune Haako](/wiki/Rune_Haako "Rune Haako"), [Poggle the Lesser](/wiki/Poggle_the_Lesser "Poggle the Lesser"), Jango Fett, and Boba Fett watch the start of the planned execution. The trio are forced to battle a [reek](/wiki/Reek "Reek"), a [nexu](/wiki/Nexu "Nexu"), and an [acklay](/wiki/Acklay "Acklay") while in chains. During their struggle, Mace Windu arrives with his Jedi strike team, and they [battle](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis") Dooku's droid army in the arena. Upon seeing so many Jedi in one place, Jango Fett jetpacks down to the arena floor and engages Windu. After a short struggle, Windu [kills](/wiki/Death "Death") Jango due to his jetpack malfunctioning. While the Jedi put up a fight, they are eventually overwhelmed by the Droid Army's numerical advantage and appear to be heading into defeat. Yoda unexpectedly arrives with the Republic's new clone army, but only a handful of Jedi have survived.

 [![ and  battle each other.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/DookuVsYoda-AOTC.png/revision/latest?cb=20241012165300) [![ and  battle each other.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/DookuVsYoda-AOTC.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20241012165300)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ad/DookuVsYoda-AOTC.png/revision/latest?cb=20241012165300) 

[Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku") and [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") battle each other.

 

An even larger battle erupts outside the arena between the Republic's clone army and the Droid Army of the Confederacy of Independent Systems. Nute Gunray and Rune Haako subsequently retreat in Gunray's ship. The Clone Army gains the upper hand, which eventually leads to the Droid Army retreating. Poggle the Lesser entrusts Count Dooku with the early plans for the [Death Star](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station"). Dooku attempts to escape, but Obi-Wan and Anakin track him to a secret hangar. Anakin immediately disobeys Obi-Wan's orders to take Dooku together and rushes at Dooku, who fires [Force lightning](/wiki/Force_lightning "Force lightning") at Anakin, tossing him to the side to some rocks and knocking him unconscious temporarily. Obi-Wan circles Dooku cautiously, the latter saying that his powers are far beyond Obi-Wan's and subsequently firing force lightning at him, Obi-Wan blocking it with his lightsaber and saying that he does not think so as Dooku ignites his curved hilted crimson red lightsaber. Obi-Wan rushes at Dooku, engaging him in a lightsaber duel. Unfortunately, while Obi-Wan is powerful, he is no match for Dooku who taunts him that Master Yoda praises Obi-Wan greatly and that he is disappointed in Obi-Wan's lack of skill. The battle lasts around half a minute as Obi-Wan is defeated. Dooku swings his blade high over his head and brings it down as Anakin, who had just awoken from being tossed to the rocks, leaped foward and blocked Dooku's killing strike on Obi-Wan, engaging Dooku, who toyed with him for several minutes before slicing off Anakin's right hand and force pushing it to the ground next to the defeated Obi-Wan. Dooku puts away his lightsaber. Yoda appears just as Dooku is about to escape, and the two masters of the Force go head-to-head in a fierce battle of the force and then a lightsaber duel with Yoda using his acrobatic style and Dooku using his elegant style. Dooku, realizing he can't defeat Yoda, attempts to topple a large pillar on Obi-Wan and Anakin as a distraction. While Yoda uses the Force to divert the pillar, Dooku flees in his [solar sailer](/wiki/Solar_sailer "Solar sailer"). Flying to the Works in the [Industrial sector](/wiki/Industrial_District "Industrial District") of Coruscant, he meets up with his master, Darth Sidious, who is pleased that the [war](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars") has begun as planned.

In the Jedi Temple, Obi-Wan, Mace and Yoda ponder Dooku's warning that Darth Sidious is controlling the Senate. Yoda is hesitant to believe this, stating that the dark side is capable of creating fear and mistrust. He and Windu agree that they should nevertheless closely monitor the Senate. Meanwhile, Chancellor Palpatine and a number of senators, including [Bail Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa "Bail Prestor Organa"), oversee the launching of massive clone trooper forces.

Back at Naboo, Anakin, with a new [mechanical arm](/wiki/Cybernetics "Cybernetics"), and Padmé hold a [secret wedding](/wiki/Wedding_of_Anakin_Skywalker_and_Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Wedding of Anakin Skywalker and Padmé Amidala"), with C-3PO and [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2 "R2-D2") as the only witnesses.

## Development[]

[John Knoll](/wiki/John_Knoll "John Knoll") told *[Star Wars Insider](/wiki/Star_Wars_Insider "Star Wars Insider")* that adapting to digital cameras was the biggest challenge his team faced as production started on *Attack of the Clones*. However, the advantage of digital cameras—which could immediately play back footage whenever the team wished—became clear to Knoll, who greatly enjoyed shooting with them.[[5]](#cite_note-Speaking_Volumes-5) When he was interviewed in [2005](/wiki/2005 "2005") by [Temuera Morrison](/wiki/Temuera_Morrison "Temuera Morrison") during an episode of the *The Tem Show*, [Rick McCallum](/wiki/Rick_McCallum "Rick McCallum") stated that [New Zealand](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Zealand "wikipedia:New Zealand") was among one of their chosen filming locations prior to Australia, but due to the *The Lord of the Rings* films being filmed in New Zealand around the same time, there were going to be complications. While filming in New Zealand was going to be an issue, [Lucasfilm](/wiki/Lucasfilm "Lucasfilm") casting directors still traveled around the country, picking up several actors in New Zealand, among these being [Bodie Taylor](/wiki/Bodie_Taylor "Bodie Taylor") and [Daniel Logan](/wiki/Daniel_Logan "Daniel Logan").[[6]](#cite_note-TheTemShow-6)

In December [2001](/wiki/2001 "2001"), it was rumored that members of [\*NSYNC](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/*NSYNC "wikipedia:*NSYNC") were filmed as extras in *Attack of the Clones*.[[7]](#cite_note-TFN1-7) In the following days, the story gained momentum, and it was reported that three band members—[Joey Fatone](/wiki/Joey_Fatone "Joey Fatone"), [JC Chasez](/wiki/Joshua_Scott_Chasez "Joshua Scott Chasez"), and [Chris Kirkpatrick](/wiki/Chris_Kirkpatrick "Chris Kirkpatrick")[[8]](#cite_note-EW1-8)—were given parts as Jedi and Naboo citizens[[9]](#cite_note-IGN-9) by producer Rick McCallum.[[10]](#cite_note-Mtv-10) Lucasfilm then later confirmed the news but denied the rumors that it was done by [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas") as a favor to his daughters [Katie](/wiki/Katie_Lucas "Katie Lucas") and [Amanda](/wiki/Amanda_Lucas "Amanda Lucas"), who were fans of the band. Also, [Justin Timberlake](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Justin_Timberlake "wikipedia:Justin Timberlake") acknowledged that he and [Lance Bass](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lance_Bass "wikipedia:Lance Bass") were not involved, but that Joey Fatone's brother [Steven Fatone](/wiki/Steven_Fatone "Steven Fatone") was.[[8]](#cite_note-EW1-8) Many *Star Wars* fans reacted negatively to the news, seeing this incident as further evidence of Star Wars "selling out," similar to some Star Wars fans' reactions to Jar Jar Binks or the [Ewoks](/wiki/Ewok "Ewok").[[11]](#cite_note-IGN2-11) On January 12, 2002, a *[Saturday Night Live](/wiki/Saturday_Night_Live "Saturday Night Live")* sketch showed a satirical "first look" at *Attack of the Clones*, wherein the movie ground to a halt to allow \*NSYNC to perform an impromptu musical number entitled "I'm a Jedi Knight in these Jedi Days."[[12]](#cite_note-SNL-12) Joey Fatone later announced that the singers' parts had been cut from the film because of the negative fan reaction. However, Lucasfilm's [Lynne Hale](/wiki/Lynne_Hale "Lynne Hale") denied this, saying that it was up to Lucas, and that "the final edit of the film is what he determines it will be."[[13]](#cite_note-E-13)

## Release and reception[]

In the lead-up to release, Lucasfilm released another series of web documentaries, and experimented with other promotional tools, including [Episode II Select](/wiki/Episode_II_Select "Episode II Select") and [Ahmed Best](/wiki/Ahmed_Best "Ahmed Best")'s on-set videos.[[14]](#cite_note-14) On [May 11](/wiki/May_11 "May 11"), 2002, [TV Guide](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/TV_Guide "wikipedia:TV Guide") released [three different covers](/wiki/Gallery_of_TV_Guide_covers "Gallery of TV Guide covers") to promote the film.[[2]](#cite_note-Season_2_Directors-2)

## Adaptations and tie-in media[]

The film's [soundtrack](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones_(soundtrack) "Star Wars: Episode II Attack of the Clones (soundtrack)") was released by Sony on April 23, 2002.

A [book version](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_II_Attack_of_the_Clones_(novelization) "Star Wars: Episode II Attack of the Clones (novelization)") of the movie was written by [R. A. Salvatore](/wiki/R._A._Salvatore "R. A. Salvatore"). It includes scenes created by Salvatore and unique to the novel. The book's prologue describes Anakin, while flying to [Ansion](/wiki/Ansion "Ansion") with Obi-Wan, having a nightmare of his mother turning into glass and shattering. The following pages relate the events leading up to Shmi Skywalker's capture by Tusken Raiders and Cliegg Lars's loss of his leg while attempting to rescue her. These scenes give a more detailed insight into Shmi's life on the moisture farm and her relationships with Cliegg, Owen, Beru, and C-3PO than can be provided in the film. Interspersed with these events are scenes of Senator Amidala on Naboo prior to her departure for Coruscant to vote on the [Military Creation Act](/wiki/Military_Creation_Act "Military Creation Act"). She discusses with her sister the question of retiring from politics to start a family and receives reports about the unrest (briefly mentioned in the film) among spice miners on Naboo's moons. The book also delves more deeply than the film into the father-son relationship of Jango and Boba Fett, making Jango's death more emotionally meaningful. (However, it also has several inaccuracies concerning Jango. For example, the author referred to his Armor as grey, when it is actually white with blue accents.) The first of [the *Boba Fett* series of young adult novels](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Boba_Fett_(novel_series) "Star Wars: Boba Fett (novel series)") draws upon this material.

### Home video[]

*Star Wars Episode II: Attack of the Clones* was [released on VHS and DVD](/wiki/Star_Wars_home_video_releases "Star Wars home video releases") on November 12, 2002. The VHS included six deleted scenes and a segment of *Star Wars: Connections*. *Attack of the Clones* would be the final VHS release of any kind for *Star Wars* in the United States. As such, it is impossible to acquire a full VHS set for the Prequel Trilogy since there would not be one for *Revenge of the Sith* (though *Revenge of the Sith* did receive a VHS release in other countries such as the UK and Australia). The DVD contains [certain elements edited or added](/wiki/List_of_changes_in_Star_Wars_re-releases#2002_Star_Wars_Episode_II:_Attack_of_the_Clones_DVD "List of changes in Star Wars re-releases") by George Lucas that make the DVD a slightly different version from its theatrical release.

* Disc 1
  + DVD Menu themes based on planets from the movie: Coruscant, Kamino, and Geonosis
  + Available subtitles: English
  + Available Audio Tracks: English (Dolby Digital 5.1 EX), Spanish (Dolby Digital 2.0 Surround), French (Dolby Digital 2.0 Surround)
  + Commentary by writer-director George Lucas, producer Rick McCallum, animation director Rob Coleman, and ILM visual effects supervisors John Knoll, Roger Guyett, and sound designer Ben Burtt
  + DVD Credits with Blooper reels
  + DVD-ROM content including website archive of [HoloNet News](/wiki/HoloNet_News_(original_website) "HoloNet News (original website)")[[15]](#cite_note-HomingBeacon-15)

* Disc 2
  + Main DVD Menu's theme is based on the Jedi Library
  + Eight exclusive [deleted scenes](/wiki/Content_cut_from_Star_Wars "Content cut from Star Wars") with introductions of George Lucas, Rick McCallum, and Ben Burtt
  + "From Puppets to Pixels: Digital Characters in Episode II": all-new full-length documentary about the creation of digital characters in Episode II
  + "State of the Art: The Previsualization of Episode II": witness the vital role of the animatics team
  + "Films Are Not Released: They Escape" sound documentary
  + Three featurettes examining the story line, action scenes, and love story through behind-the-scenes footage and interviews with the cast and filmmakers
  + 12-part Web documentary
  + "Across the Stars" music video: an original composition by John Williams crafted exclusively for this DVD
  + Exclusive production photos
  + One-sheet posters
  + International outdoor campaign
  + Trailers and TV spots
  + "[R2-D2: Beneath the Dome](/wiki/R2-D2:_Beneath_the_Dome "R2-D2: Beneath the Dome")" mockumentary trailer
  + ILM visual effects breakdown montage
  + Exclusive DVD-ROM content
  + Production photo gallery
  + College Want Ads Campaign gallery Easter egg (enhanced DVD-ROM multimedia content when you click on the weblinks of any of the posters in the image gallery, featuring downloadable wallpapers and messenger icons)[[15]](#cite_note-HomingBeacon-15)
  + DVD-ROM content includes a free trial of Hyperspace

The film was released on [Blu-ray](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Blu-ray "wikipedia:Blu-ray") in [September](/wiki/September "September") [2011](/wiki/2011 "2011").[[16]](#cite_note-SWArchive-Bring_the_Complete_Collection_Home:_Star_Wars:_The_Complete_Saga_on_Blu-Ray-16)

On [April 7](/wiki/April_7 "April 7"), [2015](/wiki/2015 "2015"), the Walt Disney Studios, 20th Century Fox, and Lucasfilm jointly announced the digital releases of the six released *Star Wars* films. As Lucasfilm had retained digital distribution rights to Episodes I through III and V through VI, Walt Disney Studios Home Entertainment released *Attack of the Clones* for digital download on [April 10](/wiki/April_10 "April 10"), 2015.[[17]](#cite_note-SW-The_Star_Wars_Digital_Movie_Collection_Coming_April_10-17)

Despite the [Walt Disney Company's](/wiki/The_Walt_Disney_Company "The Walt Disney Company") [2012](/wiki/2012 "2012") purchase of Lucasfilm Ltd. and the release rights to all future *Star Wars* films, Fox was to retain original distribution rights to [*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope"), which they co-produced and co-financed, in perpetuity in all media worldwide. Fox was also to retain theatrical, nontheatrical, and home video rights worldwide for the franchise's five subsequent films, which Lucasfilm produced and financed independently, through [May](/wiki/May "May") [2020](/wiki/2020 "2020"), at which time ownership was to transfer to Disney. This complex relationship between Fox and Disney, particularly in regards to Fox's perpetual rights to Episode IV, was to create an obstacle for any future boxed set comprising all nine films.[[18]](#cite_note-Hollywood_Reporter-18) On [December 14](/wiki/December_14 "December 14"), [2017](/wiki/2017 "2017"), The Walt Disney Company announced that it was acquiring most of Fox's parent company, [21st Century Fox](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/21st_Century_Fox "wikipedia:21st Century Fox"), including the film studio and all distribution rights to *A New Hope*.[[19]](#cite_note-Acquire-19) On [March 20](/wiki/March_20 "March 20"), [2019](/wiki/2019 "2019"), the [deal](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Acquisition_of_21st_Century_Fox_by_Disney "wikipedia:Acquisition of 21st Century Fox by Disney") was officially completed.[[20]](#cite_note-20) On [April 12](/wiki/April_12 "April 12"), 2019, a Blu-ray box set containing the nine main instalments of the *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* [saga](/wiki/Star_Wars_saga "Star Wars saga") remastered in 4K was reportedly announced to be in development for a [2020](/wiki/2020 "2020") release.[[21]](#cite_note-21)
